</p>
<ol><li>wonderful, marvelous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объяснить.html>объясни́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мельчайший.html>мельча́йших</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деталь.html>дета́лях</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́маешь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:удивительный.html>удиви́тельный</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Obʺjasní mne, v melʹčájšix detáljax, počemú ty dúmaješʹ, što ty takój <b>udivítelʹnyj</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Explain to me, in the minutest detail, why you think that you're so <b>amazing</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***удивить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удивить.html>удиви́ть</a> (3477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">диви́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">divítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивить.html>удиви́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udivítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивлять.html>удивля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to astonish, to surprise, to amaze</li></ol>

***удивиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удивиться.html>удиви́ться</a> (909)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивить.html>удиви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udivítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивиться.html>удиви́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udivítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивляться.html>удивля́ться</a></b>)
</p>

***удивление.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удивление.html>удивле́ние</a> (1548)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивить.html>удиви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udivítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивление.html>удивле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udivlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивление.html>удивле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивление.html>удивле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивление.html>удивле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>astonishment, amazement, surprise, wonder (feeling that something unexpected has happened)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивлять.html>удивля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udivljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивляться.html>удивля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udivljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивиться.html>удиви́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wonder (at), to be surprised, to be amazed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удивляться.html>удивля́ться</a></b> кому́-либо/чему́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udivljátʹsja</b> komú-libo/čemú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be amazed by someone/something</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***удила.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удила.html>удила</a> (22969)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удила.html>удила́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udilá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удила.html>уди́л</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>bit (metal in horse's mouth)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удила.html>уди́ла</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udíla</span>)

***удирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удирать.html>удира́ть</a> (12277)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-дира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-dirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удирать.html>удира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удрать.html>удра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flee, to run for one's life</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***удлинять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удлинять.html>удлиня́ть</a> (28496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">удлини́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udlinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удлинять.html>удлиня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udlinjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">удлини́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lengthen, to make longer, to elongate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удлинять.html>удлиня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:черта.html>черту́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udlinjátʹ</b> čertú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to prolong/extend a line</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(term)</i> to prolong, to extend</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удобный.html>удо́бный</a> (2158)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удобный.html>удо́бный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udóbnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)удо́бнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)удо́бней</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">удо́бнейший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>comfortable, convenient
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:удобный.html>удо́бное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>udóbnoje</b> dlja kovó-libo vrémja</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">at one's convenience, at one's leisure, at a suitable date (for one's pleasure)</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:удобный.html>удо́бный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:момент.html>моме́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>udóbnyj</b> momént</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at a <b>well-chosen</b> moment</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удовлетворять.html>удовлетворя́ть</a> (10398)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удовлетворить.html>удовлетвори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udovletvorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удовлетворять.html>удовлетворя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udovletvorjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удовлетворить.html>удовлетвори́ть</a></b>)

<li>to fulfill</li>
<li>to gratify</li>
<li>to suffice</li></ol>

***удостаивавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удостаивавший.html>удоста́ивавший</a> (32237)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удостаивавший.html>удоста́ивавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udostáivavšij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удостоить.html>удосто́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udostóitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удостаивать.html>удоста́ивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udostáivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удостоить.html>удосто́ить</a></b>)
